// ==================================== Readme ====================================

// Formatting for passive lists is (generally) in order of CX boosts, then racials, followed by entry specific passives
// Formatting is made consistent to be more digestable where possible
// By searching the racials in VSC you will be able to see at a glance the separation

// Not every entry is present, the primary reason for this file's existence is passive fields, and often they're inherited desireably
// Inhteritance trees are provided as a reference to easily fetch entries from https://bg3.norbyte.dev for further customisation
// The sibling entries are generally clumped together to make customisation more accessible

// All racials including Attack of Opportunity should be perpetuated appropriately across all entries, no matter how benign
// Spellcasting modifiers and highest mental ability score should be reflecting their class archetype if one is designated
// Flaming Fist "Casters" should have both CX_Wizard_Boost and CX_Magic_Boost
// Flaming Fist "Clerics" should have both CX_Cleric_Boost and CX_Magic_Boost
// Entries with itterations for every race should be the same. E.g. MOO_Acolyte, MOO_Fanatic and MOO_Zealot having the same Cleric/Paladin adjustments.

// CX_Martial_Boost is a new field intended to mirror CX_Magic_Boost. These are given to grunt type characters in addition to other caster class archetypes. The idea here is that there's entries which may not warrent full class archetypes, these generic passives are a mid-way solution, but also allow more generic buffs to be removed from the class based configurations.

// Generic buffs: CX_Magic_Boost / CX_Martial_Boost
// Class archetypes: CX_Barbarian_Boost;CX_Barbarian_Berserker_Boost / CX_Bard_Boost / CX_Cleric_Boost / CX_Druid_Boost;CX_Druid_Moon_Boost / CX_Fighter_Boost / CX_Monk_Boost / CX_Paladin_Boost;CX_Paladin_Oathbreaker_Boost / CX_Ranger_Boost;CX_Ranger_Hunter_Boost / CX_Rogue_Boost / CX_Sorcerer_Boost / CX_Warlock_Boost / CX_Wizard_Boost
// Spells: CX_Spells_L1, CX_Spells_L1C / CX_Spells_L2, CX_Spells_L2C / CX_Spells_L3, CX_Spells_L3C / CX_Spells_L4, CX_Spells_L4C / CX_Spells_L5, CX_Spells_L5C / CX_Spells_L6, CX_Spells_L6C

// ==================================== Other ====================================

// "_Base"
//  ├─ "_Humanoid"
//  │   ├─ "Bandit"

new entry "Bandit"
type "Character"
using "Bandit"
